constant.Debian {\n   169→\t\tif kernelVersion == \"\" {\n   170→\t\t\tlogging.Log.Warn(\"X-Vuls-Kernel-Version is empty. skip kernel vulnerability detection.\")\n   171→\t\t} else {\n   172→\t\t\tif _, err := debver.NewVersion(kernelVersion); err != nil {\n   173→\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Warnf(\"X-Vuls-Kernel-Version is invalid. skip kernel vulnerability detection. actual kernelVersion: %s, err: %s\", kernelVersion, err)\n   174→\t\t\t\tkernelVersion = \"\"\n   175→\t\t\t}\n   176→\t\t}\n   177→\t}\n   178→\n   179→\tserverName := header.Get(\"X-Vuls-Server-Name\")\n   180→\tif toLocalFile && serverName == \"\" {\n   181→\t\treturn models.ScanResult{}, errServerNameHeader\n   182→\t}\n   183→\n   184→\tdistro := config.Distro{\n   185→\t\tFamily:  family,\n   186→\t\tRelease: release,\n   187→\t}\n   188→\n   189→\tkernel := models.Kernel{\n   190→\t\tRelease: kernelRelease,\n   191→\t\tVersion: kernelVersion,\n   192→\t}\n   193→\tinstalledPackages, srcPackages, err := ParseInstalledPkgs(distro, kernel, body)\n   194→\tif err != nil {\n   195→\t\treturn models.ScanResult{}, err\n   196→\t}\n   197→\n   198→\treturn models.ScanResult{\n   199→\t\tServerName: serverName,\n   200→\t\tFamily:     family,\n   201→\t\tRelease:    release,\n   202→\t\tRunningKernel: models.Kernel{\n   203→\t\t\tRelease: kernelRelease,\n   204→\t\t\tVersion: kernelVersion,\n   205→\t\t},\n   206→\t\tPackages:    installedPackages,\n   207→\t\tSrcPackages: srcPackages,\n   208→\t\tScannedCves: models.VulnInfos{},\n   209→\t}, nil\n   210→}\n   211→\n   212→// ParseInstalledPkgs parses installed pkgs line\n   213→func ParseInstalledPkgs(distro config.Distro, kernel models.Kernel, pkgList string) (models.Packages, models.SrcPackages, error) {\n   214→\tbase := base{\n   215→\t\tDistro: distro,\n   216→\t\tosPackages: osPackages{\n   217→\t\t\tKernel: kernel,\n   218→\t\t},\n   219→\t\tlog: logging.Log,\n   220→\t}\n   221→\n   222→\tvar osType osTypeInterface\n   223→\tswitch distro.Family {\n   224→\tcase constant.Debian, constant.Ubuntu, constant.Raspbian:\n   225→\t\tosType = &debian{base: base}\n   226→\tcase constant.RedHat:\n   227→\t\tosType = &rhel{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   228→\tcase constant.CentOS:\n   229→\t\tosType = &centos{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   230→\tcase constant.Alma:\n   231→\t\tosType = &alma{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   232→\tcase constant.Rocky:\n   233→\t\tosType = &rocky{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   234→\tcase constant.Oracle:\n   235→\t\tosType = &oracle{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   236→\tcase constant.Amazon:\n   237→\t\tosType = &amazon{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   238→\tcase constant.Fedora:\n   239→\t\tosType = &fedora{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   240→\tcase constant.OpenSUSE, constant.OpenSUSELeap, constant.SUSEEnterpriseServer, constant.SUSEEnterpriseDesktop:\n   241→\t\tosType = &suse{redhatBase: redhatBase{base: base}}\n   242→\tdefault:\n   243→\t\treturn models.Packages{}, models.SrcPackages{}, xerrors.Errorf(\"Server mode for %s is not implemented yet\", base.Distro.Family)\n   244→\t}\n   245→\n   246→\treturn osType.parseInstalledPackages(pkgList)\n   247→}\n   248→\n   249→// initServers detect the kind of OS distribution of target servers\n   250→func (s Scanner) initServers() error {\n   251→\thosts, errHosts := s.detectServerOSes()\n   252→\tif len(hosts) == 0 {\n   253→\t\treturn xerrors.New(\"No scannable host OS\")\n   254→\t}\n   255→\n   256→\t// to generate random color for logging\n   257→\trand.Seed(time.Now().UnixNano())\n   258→\tfor _, srv := range hosts {\n   259→\t\tsrv.setLogger(logging.NewCustomLogger(s.Debug, s.Quiet, s.LogToFile, s.LogDir, config.Colors[rand.Intn(len(config.Colors))], srv.getServerInfo().GetServerName()))\n   260→\t}\n   261→\n   262→\tcontainers, errContainers := s.detectContainerOSes(hosts)\n   263→\tfor _, srv := range containers {\n   264→\t\tsrv.setLogger(logging.NewCustomLogger(s.Debug, s.Quiet, s.LogToFile, s.LogDir, config.Colors[rand.Intn(len(config.Colors))], srv.getServerInfo().GetServerName()))\n   265→\t}\n   266→\n   267→\t// set to pkg global variable\n   268→\tfor _, host := range hosts {\n   269→\t\tif !host.getServerInfo().ContainersOnly {\n   270→\t\t\tservers = append(servers, host)\n   271→\t\t}\n   272→\t}\n   273→\tservers = append(servers, containers...)\n   274→\terrServers = append(errHosts, errContainers...)\n   275→\n   276→\tif len(servers) == 0 {\n   277→\t\treturn xerrors.New(\"No scannable servers\")\n   278→\t}\n   279→\treturn nil\n   280→}\n   281→\n   282→func (s Scanner) detectServerOSes() (servers, errServers []osTypeInterface) {\n   283→\tlogging.Log.Info(\"Detecting OS of servers... \")\n   284→\tosTypeChan := make(chan osTypeInterface, len(s.Targets))\n   285→\tdefer close(osTypeChan)\n   286→\tfor _, target := range s.Targets {\n   287→\t\tgo func(srv config.ServerInfo) {\n   288→\t\t\tdefer func() {\n   289→\t\t\t\tif p := recover(); p != nil {\n   290→\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Panic: %s on %s\", p, srv.ServerName)\n   291→\t\t\t\t}\n   292→\t\t\t}()\n   293→\t\t\tif err := validateSSHConfig(&srv); err != nil {\n   294→\t\t\t\tcheckOS := unknown{base{ServerInfo: srv}}\n   295→\t\t\t\tcheckOS.setErrs([]error{err})\n   296→\t\t\t\tosTypeChan <- &checkOS\n   297→\t\t\t\treturn\n   298→\t\t\t}\n   299→\t\t\tosTypeChan <- s.detectOS(srv)\n   300→\t\t}(target)\n   301→\t}\n   302→\n   303→\ttimeout := time.After(time.Duration(s.TimeoutSec) * time.Second)\n   304→\tfor i := 0; i < len(s.Targets); i++ {\n   305→\t\tselect {\n   306→\t\tcase res := <-osTypeChan:\n   307→\t\t\tif 0 < len(res.getErrs()) {\n   308→\t\t\t\terrServers = append(errServers, res)\n   309→\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Errorf(\"(%d/%d) Failed: %s, err: %+v\", i+1, len(s.Targets), res.getServerInfo().ServerName, res.getErrs())\n   310→\t\t\t} else {\n   311→\t\t\t\tservers = append(servers, res)\n   312→\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Infof(\"(%d/%d) Detected: %s: %s\", i+1, len(s.Targets), res.getServerInfo().ServerName, res.getDistro())\n   313→\t\t\t}\n   314→\t\tcase <-timeout:\n   315→\t\t\tmsg := \"Timed out while detecting servers\"\n   316→\t\t\tlogging.Log.Error(msg)\n   317→\t\t\tfor servername, sInfo := range s.Targets {\n   318→\t\t\t\tfound := false\n   319→\t\t\t\tfor _, o := range append(servers, errServers...) {\n   320→\t\t\t\t\tif servername == o.getServerInfo().ServerName {\n   321→\t\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n   322→\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   323→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   324→\t\t\t\t}\n   325→\t\t\t\tif !found {\n   326→\t\t\t\t\tu := &unknown{}\n   327→\t\t\t\t\tu.setServerInfo(sInfo)\n   328→\t\t\t\t\tu.setErrs([]error{xerrors.New(\"Timed out\")})\n   329→\t\t\t\t\terrServers = append(errServers, u)\n   330→\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Errorf(\"(%d/%d) Timed out: %s\", i+1, len(s.Targets), servername)\n   331→\t\t\t\t}\n   332→\t\t\t}\n   333→\t\t}\n   334→\t}\n   335→\treturn\n   336→}\n   337→\n   338→func validateSSHConfig(c *config.ServerInfo) error {\n   339→\tif isLocalExec(c.Port, c.Host) || c.Type == constant.ServerTypePseudo {\n   340→\t\treturn nil\n   341→\t}\n   342→\n   343→\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Validating SSH Settings for Server:%s ...\", c.GetServerName())\n   344→\n   345→\tsshBinaryPath, err := ex.LookPath(\"ssh\")\n   346→\tif err != nil {\n   347→\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to lookup ssh binary path. err: %w\", err)\n   348→\t}\n   349→\n   350→\tsshConfigCmd := buildSSHConfigCmd(sshBinaryPath, c)\n   351→\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Executing... %s\", strings.Replace(sshConfigCmd, \"\\n\", \"\", -1))\n   352→\tconfigResult := localExec(*c, sshConfigCmd, noSudo)\n   353→\tif !configResult.isSuccess() {\n   354→\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to print SSH configuration. err: %w\", configResult.Error)\n   355→\t}\n   356→\tsshConfig := parseSSHConfiguration(configResult.Stdout)\n   357→\tc.User = sshConfig.user\n   358→\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Setting SSH User:%s for Server:%s ...\", sshConfig.user, c.GetServerName())\n   359→\tc.Port = sshConfig.port\n   360→\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Setting SSH Port:%s for Server:%s ...\", sshConfig.port, c.GetServerName())\n   361→\tif c.User == \"\" || c.Port == \"\" {\n   362→\t\treturn xerrors.New(\"Failed to find User or Port setting. Please check the User or Port settings for SSH\")\n   363→\t}\n   364→\n   365→\tif sshConfig.strictHostKeyChecking == \"false\" {\n   366→\t\treturn nil\n   367→\t}\n   368→\tif sshConfig.proxyCommand != \"\" || sshConfig.proxyJump != \"\" {\n   369→\t\tlogging.Log.Debug(\"known_host check under Proxy is not yet implemented\")\n   370→\t\treturn nil\n   371→\t}\n   372→\n   373→\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Checking if the host's public key is in known_hosts...\")\n   374→\tknownHostsPaths := []string{}\n   375→\tfor _, knownHost := range append(sshConfig.userKnownHosts, sshConfig.globalKnownHosts...) {\n   376→\t\tif knownHost != \"\" && knownHost != \"/dev/null\" {\n   377→\t\t\tknownHostsPaths = append(knownHostsPaths, knownHost)\n   378→\t\t}\n   379→\t}\n   380→\tif len(knownHostsPaths) == 0 {\n   381→\t\treturn xerrors.New(\"Failed to find any known_hosts to use. Please check the UserKnownHostsFile and GlobalKnownHostsFile settings for SSH\")\n   382→\t}\n   383→\n   384→\tsshKeyscanBinaryPath, err := ex.LookPath(\"ssh-keyscan\")\n   385→\tif err != nil {\n   386→\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to lookup ssh-keyscan binary path. err: %w\", err)\n   387→\t}\n   388→\tsshScanCmd := strings.Join([]string{sshKeyscanBinaryPath, \"-p\", c.Port, sshConfig.hostname}, \" \")\n   389→\tr := localExec(*c, sshScanCmd, noSudo)\n   390→\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   391→\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to ssh-keyscan. cmd: %s, err: %w\", sshScanCmd, r.Error)\n   392→\t}\n   393→\tserverKeys := parseSSHScan(r.Stdout)\n   394→\n   395→\tsshKeygenBinaryPath, err := ex.LookPath(\"ssh-keygen\")\n   396→\tif err != nil {\n   397→\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to lookup ssh-keygen binary path. err: %w\", err)\n   398→\t}\n   399→\tfor _, knownHosts := range knownHostsPaths {\n   400→\t\tvar hostname string\n   401→\t\tif sshConfig.hostKeyAlias != \"\" {\n   402→\t\t\thostname = sshConfig.hostKeyAlias\n   403→\t\t} else {\n   404→\t\t\tif c.Port != \"\" && c.Port != \"22\" {\n   405→\t\t\t\thostname = fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"[%s]:%s\\\"\", sshConfig.hostname, c.Port)\n   406→\t\t\t} else {\n   407→\t\t\t\thostname = sshConfig.hostname\n   408→\t\t\t}\n   409→\t\t}\n   410→\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"%s -F %s -f %s\", sshKeygenBinaryPath, hostname, knownHosts)\n   411→\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Executing... %s\", strings.Replace(cmd, \"\\n\", \"\", -1))\n   412→\t\tif r := localExec(*c, cmd, noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n   413→\t\t\tkeyType, clientKey, err := parseSSHKeygen(r.Stdout)\n   414→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   415→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to parse ssh-keygen result. stdout: %s, err: %w\", r.Stdout, r.Error)\n   416→\t\t\t}\n   417→\t\t\tif serverKey, ok := serverKeys[keyType]; ok && serverKey == clientKey {\n   418→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   419→\t\t\t}\n   420→\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to find the server key that matches the key registered in the client. The server key may have been changed. Please exec `$ %s` and `$ %s` or `$ %s`\",\n   421→\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s -R %s -f %s\", sshKeygenBinaryPath, hostname, knownHosts),\n   422→\t\t\t\tstrings.Join(buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath, c, nil), \" \"),\n   423→\t\t\t\tbuildSSHKeyScanCmd(sshKeyscanBinaryPath, c.Port, knownHostsPaths[0], sshConfig))\n   424→\t\t}\n   425→\t}\n   426→\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to find the host in known_hosts. Please exec `$ %s` or `$ %s`\",\n   427→\t\tstrings.Join(buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath, c, nil), \" \"),\n   428→\t\tbuildSSHKeyScanCmd(sshKeyscanBinaryPath, c.Port, knownHostsPaths[0], sshConfig))\n   429→}\n   430→\n   431→func buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath string, c *config.ServerInfo, options []string) []string {\n   432→\tcmd := []string{sshBinaryPath}\n   433→\tif len(options) > 0 {\n   434→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, options...)\n   435→\t}\n   436→\tif c.SSHConfigPath != \"\" {\n   437→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-F\", c.SSHConfigPath)\n   438→\t}\n   439→\tif c.KeyPath != \"\" {\n   440→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-i\", c.KeyPath)\n   441→\t}\n   442→\tif c.Port != \"\" {\n   443→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-p\", c.Port)\n   444→\t}\n   445→\tif c.User != \"\" {\n   446→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-l\", c.User)\n   447→\t}\n   448→\tif len(c.JumpServer) > 0 {\n   449→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-J\", strings.Join(c.JumpServer, \",\"))\n   450→\t}\n   451→\tcmd = append(cmd, c.Host)\n   452→\treturn cmd\n   453→}\n   454→\n   455→func buildSSHConfigCmd(sshBinaryPath string, c *config.ServerInfo) string {\n   456→\treturn strings.Join(buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath, c, []string{\"-G\"}), \" \")\n   457→}\n   458→\n   459→func buildSSHKeyScanCmd(sshKeyscanBinaryPath, port, knownHosts string, sshConfig sshConfiguration) string {\n   460→\tcmd := []string{sshKeyscanBinaryPath}\n   461→\tif sshConfig.hashKnownHosts == \"yes\" {\n   462→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-H\")\n   463→\t}\n   464→\tif port != \"\" {\n   465→\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-p\", port)\n   466→\t}\n   467→\treturn strings.Join(append(cmd, sshConfig.hostname, \">>\", knownHosts), \" \")\n   468→}\n   469→\n   470→type sshConfiguration struct {\n   471→\thostname              string\n   472→\thostKeyAlias          string\n   473→\thashKnownHosts        string\n   474→\tuser                  string\n   475→\tport                  string\n   476→\tstrictHostKeyChecking string\n   477→\tglobalKnownHosts      []string\n   478→\tuserKnownHosts        []string\n   479→\tproxyCommand          string\n   480→\tproxyJump             string\n   481→}\n   482→\n   483→func parseSSHConfiguration(stdout string) sshConfiguration {\n   484→\tsshConfig := sshConfiguration{}\n   485→\tfor _, line := range strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\") {\n   486→\t\tswitch {\n   487→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"user \"):\n   488→\t\t\tsshConfig.user = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"user \")\n   489→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"hostname \"):\n   490→\t\t\tsshConfig.hostname = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"hostname \")\n   491→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"hostkeyalias \"):\n   492→\t\t\tsshConfig.hostKeyAlias = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"hostkeyalias \")\n   493→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"hashknownhosts \"):\n   494→\t\t\tsshConfig.hashKnownHosts = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"hashknownhosts \")\n   495→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"port \"):\n   496→\t\t\tsshConfig.port = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"port \")\n   497→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"stricthostkeychecking \"):\n   498→\t\t\tsshConfig.strictHostKeyChecking = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"stricthostkeychecking \")\n   499→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"globalknownhostsfile \"):\n   500→\t\t\tsshConfig.globalKnownHosts = strings.Split(strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"globalknownhostsfile \"), \" \")\n   501→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"userknownhostsfile \"):\n   502→\t\t\tsshConfig.userKnownHosts = strings.Split(strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"userknownhostsfile \"), \" \")\n   503→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"proxycommand \"):\n   504→\t\t\tsshConfig.proxyCommand = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"proxycommand \")\n   505→\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"proxyjump \"):\n   506→\t\t\tsshConfig.proxyJump = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"proxyjump \")\n   507→\t\t}\n   508→\t}\n   509→\treturn sshConfig\n   510→}\n   511→\n   512→func parseSSHScan(stdout string) map[string]string {\n   513→\tkeys := map[string]string{}\n   514→\tfor _, line := range strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\") {\n   515→\t\tif line == \"\" || strings.HasPrefix(line, \"# \") {\n   516→\t\t\tcontinue\n   517→\t\t}\n   518→\t\tif ss := strings.Split(line, \" \"); len(ss) == 3 {\n   519→\t\t\tkeys[ss[1]] = ss[2]\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\t}\n   522→\treturn keys\n   523→}\n   524→\n   525→func parseSSHKeygen(stdout string) (string, string, error) {\n   526→\tfor _, line := range strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\") {\n   527→\t\tif line == \"\" || strings.HasPrefix(line, \"# \") {\n   528→\t\t\tcontinue\n   529→\t\t}\n   530→\n   531→\t\t// HashKnownHosts yes\n   532→\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(line, \"|1|\") {\n   533→\t\t\tss := strings.Split(line, \"|\")\n   534→\t\t\tif ss := strings.Split(ss[len(ss)-1], \" \"); len(ss) == 3 {\n   535→\t\t\t\treturn ss[1], ss[2], nil\n   536→\t\t\t}\n   537→\t\t} else {\n   538→\t\t\tif ss := strings.Split(line, \" \"); len(ss) == 3 {\n   539→\t\t\t\treturn ss[1], ss[2], nil\n   540→\t\t\t}\n   541→\t\t}\n   542→\t}\n   543→\treturn \"\", \"\", xerrors.New(\"Failed to parse ssh-keygen result. err: public key not found\")\n   544→}\n   545→\n   546→func (s Scanner) detectContainerOSes(hosts []osTypeInterface) (actives, inactives []osTypeInterface) {\n   547→\tlogging.Log.Info(\"Detecting OS of containers... \")\n   548→\tosTypesChan := make(chan []osTypeInterface, len(hosts))\n   549→\tdefer close(osTypesChan)\n   550→\tfor _, host := range hosts {\n   551→\t\tgo func(h osTypeInterface) {\n   552→\t\t\tdefer func() {\n   553→\t\t\t\tif p := recover(); p != nil {\n   554→\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Panic: %s on %s\",\n   555→\t\t\t\t\t\tp, h.getServerInfo().GetServerName())\n   556→\t\t\t\t}\n   557→\t\t\t}()\n   558→\t\t\tosTypesChan <- s.detectContainerOSesOnServer(h)\n   559→\t\t}(host)\n   560→\t}\n   561→\n   562→\ttimeout := time.After(time.Duration(s.TimeoutSec) * time.Second)\n   563→\tfor i := 0; i < len(hosts); i++ {\n   564→\t\tselect {\n   565→\t\tcase res := <-osTypesChan:\n   566→\t\t\tfor _, osi := range res {\n   567→\t\t\t\tsinfo := osi.getServerInfo()\n   568→\t\t\t\tif 0 < len(osi.getErrs()) {\n   569→\t\t\t\t\tinactives = append(inactives, osi)\n   570→\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Errorf(\"Failed: %s err: %+v\", sinfo.ServerName, osi.getErrs())\n   571→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   572→\t\t\t\t}\n   573→\t\t\t\tactives = append(actives, osi)\n   574→\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Infof(\"Detected: %s@%s: %s\",\n   575→\t\t\t\t\tsinfo.Container.Name, sinfo.ServerName, osi.getDistro())\n   576→\t\t\t}\n   577→\t\tcase <-timeout:\n   578→\t\t\tlogging.Log.Error(\"Some containers timed out\")\n   579→\t\t}\n   580→\t}\n   581→\treturn\n   582→}\n   583→\n   584→func (s Scanner) detectContainerOSesOnServer(containerHost osTypeInterface) (oses []osTypeInterface) {\n   585→\tcontainerHostInfo := containerHost.getServerInfo()\n   586→\tif len(containerHostInfo.ContainersIncluded) == 0 {\n   587→\t\treturn\n   588→\t}\n   589→\n   590→\trunning, err := containerHost.runningContainers()\n   591→\tif err != nil {\n   592→\t\tcontainerHost.setErrs([]error{xerrors.Errorf(\n   593→\t\t\t\"Failed to get running containers on %s. err: %w\",\n   594→\t\t\tcontainerHost.getServerInfo().ServerName, err)})\n   595→\t\treturn append(oses, containerHost)\n   596→\t}\n   597→\n   598→\tif containerHostInfo.ContainersIncluded[0] == \"${running}\" {\n   599→\t\tfor _, containerInfo := range running {\n   600→\t\t\tfound := false\n   601→\t\t\tfor _, ex := range containerHost.getServerInfo().ContainersExcluded {\n   602→\t\t\t\tif containerInfo.Name == ex || containerInfo.ContainerID == ex {\n   603→\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n   604→\t\t\t\t}\n   605→\t\t\t}\n   606→\t\t\tif found {\n   607→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   608→\t\t\t}\n   609→\n   610→\t\t\tcopied := containerHostInfo\n   611→\t\t\tcopied.SetContainer(config.Container{\n   612→\t\t\t\tContainerID: containerInfo.ContainerID,\n   613→\t\t\t\tName: s.Quiet, s.LogToFile, s.LogDir, config.Colors[rand.Intn(len(config.Colors))], srv.getServerInfo().GetServerName()))\n\t}\n\n\t// set to pkg global variable\n\tfor _, host := range hosts {\n\t\tif !host.getServerInfo().ContainersOnly {\n\t\t\tservers = append(servers, host)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tservers = append(servers, containers...)\n\terrServers = append(errHosts, errContainers...)\n\n\tif len(servers) == 0 {\n\t\treturn xerrors.New(\"No scannable servers\")\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (s Scanner) detectServerOSes() (servers, errServers []osTypeInterface) {\n\tlogging.Log.Info(\"Detecting OS of servers... \")\n\tosTypeChan := make(chan osTypeInterface, len(s.Targets))\n\tdefer close(osTypeChan)\n\tfor _, target := range s.Targets {\n\t\tgo func(srv config.ServerInfo) {\n\t\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\t\tif p := recover(); p != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Panic: %s on %s\", p, srv.ServerName)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}()\n\t\t\tif err := validateSSHConfig(&srv); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tcheckOS := unknown{base{ServerInfo: srv}}\n\t\t\t\tcheckOS.setErrs([]error{err})\n\t\t\t\tosTypeChan <- &checkOS\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tosTypeChan <- s.detectOS(srv)\n\t\t}(target)\n\t}\n\n\ttimeout := time.After(time.Duration(s.TimeoutSec) * time.Second)\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(s.Targets); i++ {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase res := <-osTypeChan:\n\t\t\tif 0 < len(res.getErrs()) {\n\t\t\t\terrServers = append(errServers, res)\n\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Errorf(\"(%d/%d) Failed: %s, err: %+v\", i+1, len(s.Targets), res.getServerInfo().ServerName, res.getErrs())\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tservers = append(servers, res)\n\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Infof(\"(%d/%d) Detected: %s: %s\", i+1, len(s.Targets), res.getServerInfo().ServerName, res.getDistro())\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase <-timeout:\n\t\t\tmsg := \"Timed out while detecting servers\"\n\t\t\tlogging.Log.Error(msg)\n\t\t\tfor servername, sInfo := range s.Targets {\n\t\t\t\tfound := false\n\t\t\t\tfor _, o := range append(servers, errServers...) {\n\t\t\t\t\tif servername == o.getServerInfo().ServerName {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\t\t\tu := &unknown{}\n\t\t\t\t\tu.setServerInfo(sInfo)\n\t\t\t\t\tu.setErrs([]error{xerrors.New(\"Timed out\")})\n\t\t\t\t\terrServers = append(errServers, u)\n\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Errorf(\"(%d/%d) Timed out: %s\", i+1, len(s.Targets), servername)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn\n}\n\nfunc validateSSHConfig(c *config.ServerInfo) error {\n\tif isLocalExec(c.Port, c.Host) || c.Type == constant.ServerTypePseudo {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Validating SSH Settings for Server:%s ...\", c.GetServerName())\n\n\tsshBinaryPath, err := ex.LookPath(\"ssh\")\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to lookup ssh binary path. err: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tsshConfigCmd := buildSSHConfigCmd(sshBinaryPath, c)\n\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Executing... %s\", strings.Replace(sshConfigCmd, \"\\n\", \"\", -1))\n\tconfigResult := localExec(*c, sshConfigCmd, noSudo)\n\tif !configResult.isSuccess() {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to print SSH configuration. err: %w\", configResult.Error)\n\t}\n\tsshConfig := parseSSHConfiguration(configResult.Stdout)\n\tc.User = sshConfig.user\n\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Setting SSH User:%s for Server:%s ...\", sshConfig.user, c.GetServerName())\n\tc.Port = sshConfig.port\n\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Setting SSH Port:%s for Server:%s ...\", sshConfig.port, c.GetServerName())\n\tif c.User == \"\" || c.Port == \"\" {\n\t\treturn xerrors.New(\"Failed to find User or Port setting. Please check the User or Port settings for SSH\")\n\t}\n\n\tif sshConfig.strictHostKeyChecking == \"false\" {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tif sshConfig.proxyCommand != \"\" || sshConfig.proxyJump != \"\" {\n\t\tlogging.Log.Debug(\"known_host check under Proxy is not yet implemented\")\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Checking if the host's public key is in known_hosts...\")\n\tknownHostsPaths := []string{}\n\tfor _, knownHost := range append(sshConfig.userKnownHosts, sshConfig.globalKnownHosts...) {\n\t\tif knownHost != \"\" && knownHost != \"/dev/null\" {\n\t\t\tknownHostsPaths = append(knownHostsPaths, knownHost)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif len(knownHostsPaths) == 0 {\n\t\treturn xerrors.New(\"Failed to find any known_hosts to use. Please check the UserKnownHostsFile and GlobalKnownHostsFile settings for SSH\")\n\t}\n\n\tsshKeyscanBinaryPath, err := ex.LookPath(\"ssh-keyscan\")\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to lookup ssh-keyscan binary path. err: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tsshScanCmd := strings.Join([]string{sshKeyscanBinaryPath, \"-p\", c.Port, sshConfig.hostname}, \" \")\n\tr := localExec(*c, sshScanCmd, noSudo)\n\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to ssh-keyscan. cmd: %s, err: %w\", sshScanCmd, r.Error)\n\t}\n\tserverKeys := parseSSHScan(r.Stdout)\n\n\tsshKeygenBinaryPath, err := ex.LookPath(\"ssh-keygen\")\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to lookup ssh-keygen binary path. err: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tfor _, knownHosts := range knownHostsPaths {\n\t\tvar hostname string\n\t\tif sshConfig.hostKeyAlias != \"\" {\n\t\t\thostname = sshConfig.hostKeyAlias\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tif c.Port != \"\" && c.Port != \"22\" {\n\t\t\t\thostname = fmt.Sprintf(\"\\\"[%s]:%s\\\"\", sshConfig.hostname, c.Port)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\thostname = sshConfig.hostname\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"%s -F %s -f %s\", sshKeygenBinaryPath, hostname, knownHosts)\n\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Executing... %s\", strings.Replace(cmd, \"\\n\", \"\", -1))\n\t\tif r := localExec(*c, cmd, noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n\t\t\tkeyType, clientKey, err := parseSSHKeygen(r.Stdout)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to parse ssh-keygen result. stdout: %s, err: %w\", r.Stdout, r.Error)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif serverKey, ok := serverKeys[keyType]; ok && serverKey == clientKey {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to find the server key that matches the key registered in the client. The server key may have been changed. Please exec `$ %s` and `$ %s` or `$ %s`\",\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s -R %s -f %s\", sshKeygenBinaryPath, hostname, knownHosts),\n\t\t\t\tstrings.Join(buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath, c, nil), \" \"),\n\t\t\t\tbuildSSHKeyScanCmd(sshKeyscanBinaryPath, c.Port, knownHostsPaths[0], sshConfig))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to find the host in known_hosts. Please exec `$ %s` or `$ %s`\",\n\t\tstrings.Join(buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath, c, nil), \" \"),\n\t\tbuildSSHKeyScanCmd(sshKeyscanBinaryPath, c.Port, knownHostsPaths[0], sshConfig))\n}\n\nfunc buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath string, c *config.ServerInfo, options []string) []string {\n\tcmd := []string{sshBinaryPath}\n\tif len(options) > 0 {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, options...)\n\t}\n\tif c.SSHConfigPath != \"\" {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-F\", c.SSHConfigPath)\n\t}\n\tif c.KeyPath != \"\" {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-i\", c.KeyPath)\n\t}\n\tif c.Port != \"\" {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-p\", c.Port)\n\t}\n\tif c.User != \"\" {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-l\", c.User)\n\t}\n\tif len(c.JumpServer) > 0 {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-J\", strings.Join(c.JumpServer, \",\"))\n\t}\n\tcmd = append(cmd, c.Host)\n\treturn cmd\n}\n\nfunc buildSSHConfigCmd(sshBinaryPath string, c *config.ServerInfo) string {\n\treturn strings.Join(buildSSHBaseCmd(sshBinaryPath, c, []string{\"-G\"}), \" \")\n}\n\nfunc buildSSHKeyScanCmd(sshKeyscanBinaryPath, port, knownHosts string, sshConfig sshConfiguration) string {\n\tcmd := []string{sshKeyscanBinaryPath}\n\tif sshConfig.hashKnownHosts == \"yes\" {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-H\")\n\t}\n\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-p\", port)\n\t}\n\treturn strings.Join(append(cmd, sshConfig.hostname, \">>\", knownHosts), \" \")\n}\n\ntype sshConfiguration struct {\n\thostname              string\n\thostKeyAlias          string\n\thashKnownHosts        string\n\tuser                  string\n\tport                  string\n\tstrictHostKeyChecking string\n\tglobalKnownHosts      []string\n\tuserKnownHosts        []string\n\tproxyCommand          string\n\tproxyJump             string\n}\n\nfunc parseSSHConfiguration(stdout string) sshConfiguration {\n\tsshConfig := sshConfiguration{}\n\tfor _, line := range strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\") {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"user \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.user = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"user \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"hostname \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.hostname = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"hostname \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"hostkeyalias \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.hostKeyAlias = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"hostkeyalias \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"hashknownhosts \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.hashKnownHosts = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"hashknownhosts \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"port \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.port = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"port \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"stricthostkeychecking \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.strictHostKeyChecking = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"stricthostkeychecking \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"globalknownhostsfile \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.globalKnownHosts = strings.Split(strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"globalknownhostsfile \"), \" \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"userknownhostsfile \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.userKnownHosts = strings.Split(strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"userknownhostsfile \"), \" \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"proxycommand \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.proxyCommand = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"proxycommand \")\n\t\tcase strings.HasPrefix(line, \"proxyjump \"):\n\t\t\tsshConfig.proxyJump = strings.TrimPrefix(line, \"proxyjump \")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn sshConfig\n}\n\nfunc parseSSHScan(stdout string) map[string]string {\n\tkeys := map[string]string{}\n\tfor _, line := range strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\") {\n\t\tif line == \"\" || strings.HasPrefix(line, \"# \") {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif ss := strings.Split(line, \" \"); len(ss) == 3 {\n\t\t\tkeys[ss[1]] = ss[2]\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn keys\n}\n\nfunc parseSSHKeygen(stdout string) (string, string, error) {\n\tfor _, line := range strings.Split(stdout, \"\\n\") {\n\t\tif line == \"\" || strings.HasPrefix(line, \"# \") {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// HashKnownHosts yes\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(line, \"|1|\") {\n\t\t\tss := strings.Split(line, \"|\")\n\t\t\tif ss := strings.Split(ss[len(ss)-1], \" \"); len(ss) == 3 {\n\t\t\t\treturn ss[1], ss[2], nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tif ss := strings.Split(line, \" \"); len(ss) == 3 {\n\t\t\t\treturn ss[1], ss[2], nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn \"\", \"\", xerrors.New(\"Failed to parse ssh-keygen result. err: public key not found\")\n}\n\nfunc (s Scanner) detectContainerOSes(hosts []osTypeInterface) (actives, inactives []osTypeInterface) {\n\tlogging.Log.Info(\"Detecting OS of containers... \")\n\tosTypesChan := make(chan []osTypeInterface, len(hosts))\n\tdefer close(osTypesChan)\n\tfor _, host := range hosts {\n\t\tgo func(h osTypeInterface) {\n\t\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\t\tif p := recover(); p != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Panic: %s on %s\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\tp, h.getServerInfo().GetServerName())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}()\n\t\t\tosTypesChan <- s.detectContainerOSesOnServer(h)\n\t\t}(host)\n\t}\n\n\ttimeout := time.After(time.Duration(s.TimeoutSec) * time.Second)\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(hosts); i++ {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase res := <-osTypesChan:\n\t\t\tfor _, osi := range res {\n\t\t\t\tsinfo := osi.getServerInfo()\n\t\t\t\tif 0 < len(osi.getErrs()) {\n\t\t\t\t\tinactives = append(inactives, osi)\n\t\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Errorf(\"Failed: %s err: %+v\", sinfo.ServerName, osi.getErrs())\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tactives = append(actives, osi)\n\t\t\t\tlogging.Log.Infof(\"Detected: %s@%s: %s\",\n\t\t\t\t\tsinfo.Container.Name, sinfo.ServerName, osi.getDistro())\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase <-timeout:\n\t\t\tlogging.Log.Error(\"Some containers timed out\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn\n}\n\nfunc (s Scanner) detectContainerOSesOnServer(containerHost osTypeInterface) (oses []osTypeInterface) {\n\tcontainerHostInfo := containerHost.getServerInfo()\n\tif len(containerHostInfo.ContainersIncluded) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\trunning, err := containerHost.runningContainers()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tcontainerHost.setErrs([]error{xerrors.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"Failed to get running containers on %s. err: %w\",\n\t\t\tcontainerHost.getServerInfo().ServerName, err)})\n\t\treturn append(oses, containerHost)\n\t}\n\n\tif containerHostInfo.ContainersIncluded[0] == \"${running}\" {\n\t\tfor _, containerInfo := range running {\n\t\t\tfound := false\n\t\t\tfor _, ex := range containerHost.getServerInfo().ContainersExcluded {\n\t\t\t\tif containerInfo.Name == ex || containerInfo.ContainerID == ex {\n\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif found {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcopied := containerHostInfo\n\t\t\tcopied.SetContainer(config.Container{\n\t\t\t\tContainerID: containerInfo.ContainerID,\n\t\t\t\tName:        containerInfo.Name,\n\t\t\t\tImage:       containerInfo.Image,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\tos := s.detectOS(copied)\n\t\t\toses = append(oses, os)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn oses\n\t}\n\n\texitedContainers, err := containerHost.exitedContainers()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tcontainerHost.setErrs([]error{xerrors.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"Failed to get exited containers on %s. err: %w\",\n\t\t\tcontainerHost.getServerInfo().ServerName, err)})\n\t\treturn append(oses, containerHost)\n\t}\n\n\tvar exited, unknown []string\n\tfor _, container := range containerHostInfo.ContainersIncluded {\n\t\tfound := false\n\t\tfor _, c := range running {\n\t\t\tif c.ContainerID == container || c.Name == container {\n\t\t\t\tcopied := containerHostInfo\n\t\t\t\tcopied.SetContainer(c)\n\t\t\t\tos := s.detectOS(copied)\n\t\t\t\toses = append(oses, os)\n\t\t\t\tfound = true\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\tfoundInExitedContainers := false\n\t\t\tfor _, c := range exitedContainers {\n\t\t\t\tif c.ContainerID == container || c.Name == container {\n\t\t\t\t\texited = append(exited, container)\n\t\t\t\t\tfoundInExitedContainers = true\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif !foundInExitedContainers {\n\t\t\t\tunknown = append(unknown, container)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif 0 < len(exited) || 0 < len(unknown) {\n\t\tcontainerHost.setErrs([]error{xerrors.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"Some containers on %s are exited or unknown. exited: %s, unknown: %s\",\n\t\t\tcontainerHost.getServerInfo().ServerName, exited, unknown)})\n\t\treturn append(oses, containerHost)\n\t}\n\treturn oses\n}\n\nfunc (s Scanner) detectOS(c config.ServerInfo) osTypeInterface {\n\tif itsMe, osType, _ := detectPseudo(c); itsMe {\n\t\treturn osType\n\t}\n\n\tif itsMe, osType, fatalErr := s.detectDebianWithRetry(c); fatalErr != nil {\n\t\tosType.setErrs([]error{xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to detect OS: %w\", fatalErr)})\n\t\treturn osType\n\t} else if itsMe {\n\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Debian based Linux. Host: %s:%s\", c.Host, c.Port)\n\t\treturn osType\n\t}\n\n\tif itsMe, osType := detectRedhat(c); itsMe {\n\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Redhat based Linux. Host: %s:%s\", c.Host, c.Port)\n\t\treturn osType\n\t}\n\n\tif itsMe, osType := detectSUSE(c); itsMe {\n\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"SUSE Linux. Host: %s:%s\", c.Host, c.Port)\n\t\treturn osType\n\t}\n\n\tif itsMe, osType := detectFreebsd(c); itsMe {\n\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"FreeBSD. Host: %s:%s\", c.Host, c.Port)\n\t\treturn osType\n\t}\n\n\tif itsMe, osType := detectAlpine(c); itsMe {\n\t\tlogging.Log.Debugf(\"Alpine. Host: %s:%s\", c.Host, c.Port)\n\t\treturn osType\n\t}\n\n\tosType := &unknown{base{ServerInfo: c}}\n\tosType.setErrs([]error{xerrors.New(\"Unknown OS Type\")})\n\treturn osType\n}\n\n// Retry as it may stall on the first SSH connection\n// https://github.com/future-architect/vuls/pull/753\nfunc (s Scanner) detectDebianWithRetry(c config.ServerInfo) (itsMe bool, deb osTypeInterface, err error) {\n\ttype Response struct {\n\t\titsMe bool\n\t\tdeb   osTypeInterface\n\t\terr   error\n\t}\n\tresChan := make(chan Response, 1)\n\tgo func(c config.ServerInfo) {\n\t\titsMe, osType, fatalErr := detectDebian(c)\n\t\tresChan <- Response{itsMe, osType, fatalErr}\n\t}(c)\n\n\ttimeout := time.After(time.Duration(3) * time.Second)\n\tselect {\n\tcase res := <-resChan:\n\t\treturn res.itsMe, res.deb, res.err\n\tcase <-timeout:\n\t\ttime.Sleep(100 * time.Millisecond)\n\t\treturn detectDebian(c)\n\t}\n}\n\n// checkScanModes checks scan mode\nfunc (s Scanner) checkScanModes() error {\n\tfor _, s := range servers {\n\t\tif err := s.checkScanMode(); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"servers.%s.scanMode err: %w\",\n\t\t\t\ts.getServerInfo().GetServerName(), err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// checkDependencies checks dependencies are installed on target servers.\nfunc (s Scanner) checkDependencies() {\n\tparallelExec(func(o osTypeInterface) error {\n\t\treturn o.checkDeps()\n\t}, s.TimeoutSec)\n\treturn\n}\n\n// checkIfSudoNoPasswd checks whether vuls can sudo with nopassword via SSH\nfunc (s Scanner) checkIfSudoNoPasswd() {\n\tparallelExec(func(o osTypeInterface) error {\n\t\treturn o.checkIfSudoNoPasswd()\n\t}, s.TimeoutSec)\n\treturn\n}\n\n// detectPlatform detects the platform of each servers.\nfunc (s Scanner) detectPlatform() {\n\tparallelExec(func(o osTypeInterface) error {\n\t\to.detectPlatform()\n\t\t// Logging only if platform can not be specified\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}, s.TimeoutSec)\n\n\tfor i, s := range servers {\n\t\tif s.getServerInfo().IsContainer() {\n\t\t\tlogging.Log.Infof(\"(%d/%d) %s on %s is running on %s\",\n\t\t\t\ti+1, len(servers),\n\t\t\t\ts.getServerInfo().Container.Name,\n\t\t\t\ts.getServerInfo().ServerName,\n\t\t\t\ts.getPlatform().Name,\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tlogging.Log.Infof(\"(%d/%d) %s is running on %s\",\n\t\t\t\ti+1, len(servers),\n\t\t\t\ts.getServerInfo().ServerName,\n\t\t\t\ts.getPlatform().Name,\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn\n}\n\n// detectIPS detects the IPS of each servers.\nfunc (s Scanner) detectIPS() {\n\tparallelExec(func(o osTypeInterface) error {\n\t\to.detectIPS()\n\t\t// Logging only if IPS can not be specified\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}, s.TimeoutSec)\n\n\tfor i, s := range servers {\n\t\tif !s.getServerInfo().IsContainer() {\n\t\t\tlogging.Log.Infof(\"(%d/%d) %s has %d IPS integration\",\n\t\t\t\ti+1, len(servers),\n\t\t\t\ts.getServerInfo().ServerName,\n\t\t\t\tlen(s.getServerInfo().IPSIdentifiers),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// execScan scan\nfunc (s Scanner) execScan() error {\n\tif len(servers)
